<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column6_4161b2-4c"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading6_7da03d-f5 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_7da03d-f5">Knoxville </h1>



<h1 class="kt-adv-heading6_cf8a9e-d7 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-9-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_cf8a9e-d7">Backyard &amp; Beyond</h1>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_55ede7-68 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-4-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_55ede7-68"><strong>Exploring Known And Not So Known Adventures In East Tennessee</strong></p>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id6_739313-54 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-3-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-row kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column6_61bcbc-ba inner-column-1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h6 class="kt-adv-heading6_6d526f-81 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_6d526f-81">WHAT CAN YOU FIND HERE?</h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading6_94c30e-31 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-2-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_94c30e-31">Welcome to Knoxville Backyard &amp; Beyond</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_974b99-71 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_974b99-71">We write about things to do and places to see in our hometown and East Tennessee.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_1a4591-57 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_1a4591-57">We highlight the best of Knoxville, from familiar attractions to unique local experiences, perfect for both first-time visitors and locals seeking new adventures. These are the places that we consistently return to over the years with our own families. </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_d44fa8-cc wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_d44fa8-cc">And because Knoxville is within a day&#8217;s drive of half of the continental United States, we’ve shared a variety of weekend getaway destinations that we have always enjoyed and recommend to others.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_a7a2ab-d2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_a7a2ab-d2">All of those little details that can make or break a trip? </p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_fffc0d-c5 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_fffc0d-c5"><strong>We’ve got them covered.</strong></p>
</div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column6_294690-dc inner-column-2"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column6_1d30d1-97 inner-column-3"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading6_7f3755-c9 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_7f3755-c9">Who We Are</h2>



<p>Hi! We are Amy and Amanda, two good friends who were born and raised in Knoxville.</p>



<p>Our families love to hike, camp, bike, and paddle our way around all the beautiful places in East Tennessee while also finding good food, good craft beer, and perhaps a museum or two along the way!</p>



<p>We started this blog to share our favorite places and make it easier for families to plan their own adventures.&nbsp;We have taken our own families to these museums, on these hikes, and eaten at these restaurants.&nbsp;</p>



<p>We have done the planning part for you, leaving you free to have the fun!</p>

</div></div>

<h2 class="kt-adv-heading6_e77448-0f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_e77448-0f">Backyard</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_d039f0-26 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_d039f0-26">Explore the Urban Wilderness, greenways in Maryville, museums in Oak Ridge, Norris Dam State Park, East Knoxville gems, and so much more right in Knoxville’s backyard!</p>

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column6_d9dda1-c7"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h6 class="kt-adv-heading6_c687dc-98 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_c687dc-98">Need Ideas? Too Busy To Research A Trip?</h6>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading6_fc49da-18 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_fc49da-18">Weekend Getaway Guides</h2>



<p>We love to explore awesome destinations within a few hours by car from Knoxville. These are our tried and true trips taken with our own families, we don’t write about places we haven’t been. Where to stay, where to eat, and where to play – it’s all here!</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns6_b7b504-1d"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn6_4d3879-84 kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill  kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://backyardknoxville.com/weekend-getaways/"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Explore Our Weekend Getaway Ideas!</span></a></div>



<p><strong>WE BELIEVE KIDS AND THE OUTDOORS GO HAND IN HAND</strong></p>



<p>You’ll find lots of fresh air options in our blogs and guides. Our favorite hikes, bike rides, playgrounds, historic sites, float trips, and more — all kid-tested and approved as well as fun for adults too</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading6_700572-2e wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading6_700572-2e"><strong>WE INCLUDE LOCAL FOOD RECOMMENDATIONS</strong></p>



<p>We are always in search of good local food. This could mean a food truck,&nbsp;a pizza place, or a nice sit-down restaurant, but always delicious.&nbsp;Likewise, if there are any local brews, wines, or coffee houses around, we’ll mention those too.</p>
